\item\contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_unity_engine_1_1_test_tools_1_1_unity_set_up_attribute}{Unity\+Engine.\+Test\+Tools.\+Unity\+Set\+Up\+Attribute}} \\*The {\ttfamily Unity\+Set\+Up} and Unity\+Tear\+Down\+Attribute attributes are identical to the standard {\ttfamily Set\+Up} and {\ttfamily Tear\+Down} attributes, with the exception that they allow for IEdit\+Mode\+Test\+Yield\+Instruction. \item\contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_unity_engine_1_1_test_tools_1_1_unity_tear_down_attribute}{Unity\+Engine.\+Test\+Tools.\+Unity\+Tear\+Down\+Attribute}} \\*The Unity\+Set\+Up\+Attribute and {\ttfamily Unity\+Tear\+Down} attributes are identical to the standard {\ttfamily Set\+Up} and {\ttfamily Tear\+Down} attributes, with the exception that they allow for IEdit\+Mode\+Test\+Yield\+Instruction. The {\ttfamily Unity\+Set\+Up} and {\ttfamily Unity\+Tear\+Down} attributes expect a return type of \href{https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.collections.ienumerator?view=netframework-4.8}{\texttt{ IEnumerator}}. }{\pageref{class_unity_engine_1_1_test_tools_1_1_unity_tear_down_attribute}}{}
\item\contentsline{section}{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_unity_engine_1_1_test_tools_1_1_unity_test_attribute}{Unity\+Engine.\+Test\+Tools.\+Unity\+Test\+Attribute}} \\*{\ttfamily Unity\+Test} attribute is the main addition to the standard \href{http://www.nunit.org/}{\texttt{ NUnit}} library for the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} Test Framework. This type of unit test allows you to skip a frame from within a test (so background tasks can finish) or give certain commands to the \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} {\bfseries{Editor}}, such as performing a domain reload or entering {\bfseries{Play Mode}} from an {\bfseries{Edit Mode}} test. In Play Mode, the {\ttfamily Unity\+Test} attribute runs as a \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/Manual/Coroutines.html}{\texttt{ coroutine}}. Whereas Edit Mode tests run in the \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/ScriptReference/EditorApplication-update.html}{\texttt{ Editor\+Application.\+update}} callback loop. The {\ttfamily Unity\+Test} attribute is, in fact, an alternative to the {\ttfamily NUnit} \href{https://github.com/nunit/docs/wiki/Test-Attribute}{\texttt{ Test attribute}}, which allows yielding instructions back to the framework. Once the instruction is complete, the test run continues. If you {\ttfamily yield return null}, you skip a frame. That might be necessary to ensure that some changes do happen on the next iteration of either the {\ttfamily Editor\+Application.\+update} loop or the \href{https://docs.unity3d.com/Manual/ExecutionOrder.html}{\texttt{ game loop}}. }{\pageref{class_unity_engine_1_1_test_tools_1_1_unity_test_attribute}}{}
